 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh on Tuesday stressed on restoring the dignity of the holy Ganges river and said that immediate steps should be taken in this direction
 pradhanmantri rashtriya ganga nadi basin praadhikaran kii baithak ko sambodhit kar rahe the
 He said that there is a need to take immediate and effective steps to restore the dignity of the river Ganga, which provides water to 40 percent of the country's population in 11 states
 pradhanmantri ne mana ki ganga nadi kaa sangrakshan ek jatil kaam he, jise hinduon ne devi kaa darja de rakhaa he
 He also said that earlier efforts in this direction were not very successful
 isliye bauddhik va vyaavhaarik kadam uthaane kii aavashyaktaa he, na ki tukdon main kaam karne kii jarurat he

 On Shattila Ekadashi, sesame is used in all things like bathing, offerings, food, donation, tarpan etc
 is din vyakti ko subah snaan karke bhagwaan vishnu kii tilon se puja kerani chahie

 - Face east direction with 108 fistfuls of sesame seeds 108 times and offer की Namo Bhagavate Vasudevaya Mantra
 - kisi yogya vidwaan brahman kii salaah se dakshin disha kii taraf munh karke pitaron ke liye til se tarpan karen

 Have they become the "aging" rascals who do not want to let the command slip from their hands? Are the coin-centric technocrats who tried to bring change and get angry with many "old guardians" in this affair? Has the board of Infosys failed to fulfill the responsibility it was entrusted to it? Is there any truth within Infosys in the allegations of anonymous whistleblowers and promoters over financial malpractices and corporate governance? India Today went behind the scenes and spoke with several people involved in the incident

 inaki jagah naarad raay cabinet main liye gaye

 a photo of US President Barack Obama has gone viral on social media
 is photo main obama bijepi kii ore se pradhanmantri pad ke ummidavaar narendra modi ke bhaashan kaa video dekhte najar aa rahe hai

 haalanki ye photo farji he
 Actually, this fake photo is being spread on social media by tampering with an old picture of Obama
 vaastavik tasviir 28 janvari, 2011 kii he, tab obama misr ke tatkaaleen raashtrapati husnee mubarak ke pad chhodte samay die gaye bhaashan ko dekh rahe the

 farji tasviir main mubarak ke sthaan par modi kii tasviir laga di gai

 is farji tasviir ke neeche likhaa gaya he obama bhi sunate hai 'namo' kaa bhaashan
 Those who shared this fake picture on social media include BJP MP CR Patil from Navsari in Gujarat
 jab patil se sampark kiya gaya to unhone kaha ki unhen isaki jaankaree nahin he ki tasviir ke saath chhedchhad kii gai he

 patil ne kaha ki iske peeche bijepi ke virodhiyon kaa haath ho saktaa he

 rohit ne match ke baad kaha, yah bahut acha match tha

 ham aisa kar sakate hai or ham hameshaa is tarah ke pradarshan kii ummid karte hai

 yah vastav main shandaar pradarshan he
